</button></div> <div class="clearfix"></div> </div> <div class="col-7 col-sm-8 col-md-7 col-lg-8"><div class="jw-artist" title="Blackstreet / Ginuwine"><a data-ua_action="ln_artist" title="No Diggity"><a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/blackstreet-ginuwine-no-diggity/752594-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">No Diggity</a></div><div class="jw-label" title="Home Hitters US"><a data-ua_action="ln_label" href="/labels/Home+Hitters+US/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Home Hitters US</a></div><div class="jw-review mt-2">Blackstreet's "No Diggity" is a stone cold hip hop classic. From proper club plays to cheesy parochial nights out, it unites everyone on the dance floor and never fails to become a communal singalong. It sounds as hot now as it ever did and so makes sense for Home Hitters to serve up a new limited pressing. The b-side is from US giant Ginuwine. "Pony" was his debut single co written with Timbaland and Static Major, and it is a deep cut and libidinous tune with obvious sexual metaphors and vocodered vocal samples, a cartoon whistle slide and stop-start rhythm makes it all the more alluring. <div class="jw-review-more" onclick="this.parentNode.className += ' more'; this.remove();">...<span class="text-primary px-3">Read more</span></div></div> </div> </div> </div></div><div class="col-12 col-md-6"><div class="jw-item jw-item-review mb-4 mb-md-5"> <div class="row gutters-sm"> <div class="col-5 col-sm-4 col-md-5 col-lg-4"> <a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/cigarettes-after-sex-cry/745894-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);"> <div class="img-square mb-2 img-release"> <img alt="Cigarettes After Sex - Cry" class="lazy" data-src="https://imagescdn.juno.co.uk/300/CS745894-01A-MED.jpg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAANvf7wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw=="/><div class="jw-special">ALBUM OF THE WEEK</div></div> </a><div class="jw-format float-left">LP</div><div class="jw-actions float-right"><span class="text-cta pr-2">£17.87</span><a class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ultraplayer_play" data-ua_action="play" href="/MP3/SF745894-01-01-01.mp3" rel="nofollow" title="Listen"> <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-listen"></span> </a><button class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ml-1" data-ua_action="add to cart" onclick="uaAddEvent(event); addToCartPopup(745894, 1);" title="Add to cart"> <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-cart-add text-cta"></span> </button></div> <div class="clearfix"></div> </div> <div class="col-7 col-sm-8 col-md-7 col-lg-8"><div class="jw-artist" title="Cigarettes After Sex"><a data-ua_action="ln_artist" href="/artists/Cigarettes+After+Sex/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Cigarettes After Sex</a></div><div class="jw-title" title="Cry"><a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/cigarettes-after-sex-cry/745894-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Cry</a></div><div class="jw-label" title="Partisan"><a data-ua_action="ln_label" href="/labels/Partisan/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Partisan</a></div><div class="jw-review mt-2">With the combination of band name and album title this one's always going to be a bit of a tearjerker, packed with self-reflection and self-loathing. No regrets, though, as Greg Gonzalez muses on sensuality, the loss of those we care about, the loss of self to another and the endless yearning of the human heart. Shades of Lord Huron and a wealth of gloomy shoegazers can be felt, but even though "Cry" represents a next step for Cigarettes After Sex - edging into more minimalistic territories - it's still immediately identifiable as this band, and so won't fail to instantly resonate with avid fans. Packed with an exquisite, opiate balladry at once heartfelt and heartbroken, it's hard to tell whether this is exactly what you need to hear when living through your blue period or precisely what you shouldn't listen to. Either way, it's quiet impact is immense.<div class="jw-review-more" onclick="this.parentNode.className += ' more'; this.remove();">...<span class="text-primary px-3">Read more</span></div></div> </div> </div> </div></div><div class="col-12 col-md-6"><div class="jw-item jw-item-review mb-4 mb-md-5"> <div class="row gutters-sm"> <div class="col-5 col-sm-4 col-md-5 col-lg-4"> <a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/lanark-artefax-corra-linn/753891-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);"> <div class="img-square mb-2 img-release"> <img alt="Lanark Artefax - Corra Linn" class="lazy" data-src="https://imagescdn.juno.co.uk/300/CS753891-01A-MED.jpg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAANvf7wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw=="/></div> </a><div class="jw-format float-left">12"</div><div class="jw-actions float-right"><span class="text-cta pr-2">£10.25</span><a class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ultraplayer_play" data-ua_action="play" href="/MP3/SF753891-01-01-01.mp3" rel="nofollow" title="Listen"> <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-listen"></span> </a><button class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ml-1" data-ua_action="add to cart" onclick="uaAddEvent(event); Bass heavy and melodic, with falling keys and glassy pads raining down the face of each track, "Moo Orphaned Drift" has a cosmic air to it while opening cut "Corra Linn" is an IDM drum flurry, but it is closer "Ferthenheap" which makes the most impact; it's an ambient, emotionally devastating neo-classical piano piece of the highest order.<div class="jw-review-more" onclick="this.parentNode.className += ' more'; this.remove();">...<span class="text-primary px-3">Read more</span></div></div> </div> </div> </div></div><div class="col-12 col-md-6"><div class="jw-item jw-item-review mb-4 mb-md-5"> <div class="row gutters-sm"> <div class="col-5 col-sm-4 col-md-5 col-lg-4"> <a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/space-samurais-vol-1/744490-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);"> <div class="img-square mb-2 img-release"> <img alt="Various - Space Samurai's Vol 1" class="lazy" data-src="https://imagescdn.juno.co.uk/300/CS744490-01A-MED.jpg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAANvf7wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw=="/></div> </a><div class="jw-format float-left">LP</div><div class="jw-actions float-right"><span class="text-cta pr-2">£21.25</span><a class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ultraplayer_play" data-ua_action="play" href="/MP3/SF744490-01-01-01.mp3" rel="nofollow" title="Listen"> <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-listen"></span> </a><button class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ml-1" data-ua_action="add to cart" onclick="uaAddEvent(event); addToCartPopup(744490, 1);" title="Add to cart"> <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-cart-add text-cta"></span> </button></div> <div class="clearfix"></div> </div> <div class="col-7 col-sm-8 col-md-7 col-lg-8"><div class="jw-artist" title="Various"><a data-ua_action="ln_artist" href="/artists/Various/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Various</a></div><div class="jw-title" title="Space Samurai's Vol 1"><a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/space-samurais-vol-1/744490-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Space Samurai's Vol 1</a></div><div class="jw-label" title="Childhood Intelligence"><a data-ua_action="ln_label" href="/labels/Childhood+Intelligence/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Childhood Intelligence</a></div><div class="jw-review mt-2">While the Childhood Intelligence label has previous form when it comes to offering up multi-artist EPs, little they've released to date is quite as epic, expansive and eclectic as this compilation style double-pack. There's sadly not room to list all of the highlights and subtle variations on offer - it's pretty much fire from start to finish - but our current favourites include the acid-flecked sci-fi techno of Brad P's "Theory Test Level 3", the sparse, bass-heavy shuffle of Dei Sub's "Through Flow", the dreamy but out there ambient dub flex of QWERTY's "26xm (Canal Time Shift Mix)", the 21st century clonk revivalism of Reedale Rise's ace "Capricious" and the glistening analogue electro-meets-Chicago jack pulse of Cygnus' "Vega".<div class="jw-review-more" onclick="this.parentNode.className += ' more'; this.remove();">...<span class="text-primary px-3">Read more</span></div></div> </div> </div> </div></div><div class="col-12 col-md-6"><div class="jw-item jw-item-review mb-4 mb-md-5"> <div class="row gutters-sm"> <div class="col-5 col-sm-4 col-md-5 col-lg-4"> <a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/dave-holland-zakir-hussain-chris-good-hope/744961-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);"> <div class="img-square mb-2 img-release"> <img alt="Dave Holland / Zakir Hussain / Chris Potter - Good Hope" class="lazy" data-src="https://imagescdn.juno.co.uk/300/CS744961-01A-MED.jpg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAANvf7wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw=="/></div> </a><div class="jw-format float-left">CD</div><div class="jw-actions float-right"><span class="text-cta pr-2">£9.84</span><a class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ultraplayer_play" data-ua_action="play" href="/MP3/SF744961-01-01-01.mp3" rel="nofollow" title="Listen"> <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-listen"></span> </a><button class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ml-1" data-ua_action="add to cart" onclick="uaAddEvent(event); addToCartPopup(744961, 1);" title="Add to cart"> <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-cart-add text-cta"></span> </button></div> <div class="clearfix"></div> </div> <div class="col-7 col-sm-8 col-md-7 col-lg-8"><div class="jw-artist" title="Dave Holland / Zakir Hussain / Chris Potter"><a data-ua_action="ln_artist" href="/artists/Dave+Holland/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Dave Holland</a> / <a data-ua_action="ln_artist" href="/artists/Zakir+Hussain/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Zakir Hussain</a> / <a data-ua_action="ln_artist" href="/artists/Chris+Potter/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Chris Potter</a></div><div class="jw-title" title="Good Hope"><a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/dave-holland-zakir-hussain-chris-good-hope/744961-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Good Hope</a></div><div class="jw-label" title="Edition"><a data-ua_action="ln_label" href="/labels/Edition/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Edition</a></div><div class="jw-review mt-2">It would be fair to say that Dave Holland, Zakir Hussain and Chris Potter are not your average jazz trio. For starters, we can't think of many other trios comprised of a double bassist, a tabla player and a saxophonist. It's a musical line-up that guarantees intriguing, intoxicating and exotic music, as "Good Hope" emphatically proves. There's something genuinely alluring about the trio's combination of intricate table rhythms, inventive and off-kilter double bass lines, and sax solos that wind their way around both like a fell runner zig-zagging his or her way up a windswept mountainside. It's jazz, Jim, but not as we know it.<div class="jw-review-more" onclick="this.parentNode.className += ' more'; this.remove();">...<span class="text-primary px-3">Read more</span></div></div> </div> </div> </div></div><div class="col-12 col-md-6"><div class="jw-item jw-item-review mb-4 mb-md-5"> <div class="row gutters-sm"> <div class="col-5 col-sm-4 col-md-5 col-lg-4"> <a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/roc-marciano-blizzard-two-concepts-for-the/748477-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);"> <div class="img-square mb-2 img-release"> <img alt="Roc Marciano / Damu The Fudgemunk - Blizzard: Two Concepts For The 22nd Century" class="lazy" data-src="https://imagescdn.juno.co.uk/300/CS748477-01A-MED.jpg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAANvf7wAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw=="/><div class="jw-special">LIMITED BLUE VINYL 7"</div></div> </a><div class="jw-format float-left">7"</div><div class="jw-actions float-right"><span class="text-cta pr-2">£14.99</span><a class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ultraplayer_play" data-ua_action="play" href="/MP3/SF748477-01-01-01.mp3" rel="nofollow" title="Listen"> <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-listen"></span> </a><button class="btn btn-secondary btn-xs ml-1" data-ua_action="add to cart" onclick="uaAddEvent(event); addToCartPopup(748477, 1);" title="Add to cart"> <span aria-hidden="true" class="glyphicon glyphicon-cart-add text-cta"></span> </button></div> <div class="clearfix"></div> </div> <div class="col-7 col-sm-8 col-md-7 col-lg-8"><div class="jw-artist" title="Roc Marciano / Damu The Fudgemunk"><a data-ua_action="ln_artist" href="/artists/Roc+Marciano/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Roc Marciano</a> / <a data-ua_action="ln_artist" href="/artists/Damu+The+Fudgemunk/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Damu The Fudgemunk</a></div><div class="jw-title" title="Blizzard: Two Concepts For The 22nd Century"><a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/roc-marciano-blizzard-two-concepts-for-the/748477-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Blizzard: Two Concepts For The 22nd Century</a></div><div class="jw-label" title="Redefinition US"><a data-ua_action="ln_label" href="/labels/Redefinition+US/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);">Redefinition US</a></div><div class="jw-review mt-2">To help us get ready for the harsh months ahead, ice cold Long Island MC Roc Marciano hits as hard as his boxing counterpart on this new collaboration with Damu The Fudgemunk. "Blizzard: Two Concepts For The 22nd Century" cuts deep and will transport you to the North and South poles of our hemisphere in the track's 2 distinct mixes. Of course, the production is just as key to this one's success; Fudgemunk is riding high this year after a big EP with Blu and MF Doom, and assembles some great beats and thematic scratching into the mix. With rhymes and beats this icy, you might have to store the wax in your freezer instead of the shelf.

That landed on Diggers With Gratitude who are rightfully revisiting his catalogue to make available again the tunes that have become really quite pricey. This is one of three such releases this month and focuses on "Pure Dynamite", a laid back, deep cut joint with positive vibrations and funky guitar riffs stitched into the soulful, leggy beats. "Axe Maniac" on the flip then gets busier and exudes plenty of 80s attitude. <div class="jw-review-more" onclick="this.parentNode.className += ' more'; this.remove();">...<span class="text-primary px-3">Read more</span></div></div> </div> </div> </div></div><div class="col-12 col-md-6"><div class="jw-item jw-item-review mb-4 mb-md-5"> <div class="row gutters-sm"> <div class="col-5 col-sm-4 col-md-5 col-lg-4"> <a data-ua_action="ln_product" href="/products/love-is-all-i-bring-reggae/748121-01/" onclick="uaAddEvent(event);"> <div class="img-square mb-2 img-release"> <img alt="Various - Love Is All I Bring: Reggae Hits &amp;
